    class RequestHandler {
        <<Protocol>>
        +execute() UserPreferenceResponse
    }
    class GetRequestHandler {
        -preference_repository: UserPreferenceRepository
        -request: UserPreferenceRequest
        +execute() UserPreferenceResponse
    }
    class PutRequestHandler {
        -preference_repository: UserPreferenceRepository
        -user_repository: UserRepository
        -request: UserPreferenceRequest
        +execute() UserPreferenceResponse
    }
    class UserPreferenceRepository
    class UserRepository
    class UserPreferenceRequest
    class UserPreferenceResponse {
        -user_preference
        -status_code
    }
    class DatabaseError

    RequestHandler <|.. GetRequestHandler
    RequestHandler <|.. PutRequestHandler
    GetRequestHandler --> UserPreferenceRepository : preference_repository
    GetRequestHandler --> UserPreferenceRequest : request
    GetRequestHandler --> UserPreferenceResponse : returns
    PutRequestHandler --> UserPreferenceRepository : preference_repository
    PutRequestHandler --> UserRepository : user_repository
    PutRequestHandler --> UserPreferenceRequest : request
    PutRequestHandler --> UserPreferenceResponse : returns
    PutRequestHandler ..> DatabaseError : raises
    UserRepository --> UserPreferenceRepository : uses (persona_id)

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    subgraph GET ["GetRequestHandler.execute"]
        GStart([Start])
        GGet[/"preference_repository.get(auth0_id, version)"/]
        GExists{user_preference\nexists?}
        G404([Return 404, user_preference=None])
        G200([Return 200, user_preference])
    end
    GStart --> GGet --> GExists
    GExists -- Yes --> G200
    GExists -- No --> G404

    subgraph PUT ["PutRequestHandler.execute"]
        PStart([Start])
        PPersona["user_repository.get_persona_id(auth0_id)"]
        PPersonaExists{persona_id\nfound?}
        PRaiseDb([Raise DatabaseError])
        PUpdate["preference_repository.update(auth0_id, persona_id, payload, version)"]
        PUpdated{user_preference\nreturned?}
        PCreate["preference_repository.create(auth0_id, persona_id, payload, version)"]
        PStatus201([Return 201, user_preference])
        PStatus200([Return 200, user_preference])
    end
    PStart --> PPersona --> PPersonaExists
    PPersonaExists -- No --> PRaiseDb
    PPersonaExists -- Yes --> PUpdate --> PUpdated
    PUpdated -- Yes --> PStatus200
    PUpdated -- No --> PCreate --> PStatus201

    %% Top-level entry points
    StartAll([Entry])
    StartAll --> |GET request| GStart
    StartAll --> |PUT request| PStart
```
